DCU/Department Omagh

SUBJECT Rv Maureen McKelvey

TO: D/inspector, Omagh

With reference to the attached correspondence from the DPP and the attached defence
certificate; I report as follows.

I have attached 2 copies of unused material as itemised on the schedule of unused material,
Items No 1 to 7 refer.

I have also examined the attached defence certificate and in conjunction with paragraph 4 of
the DPP letter and the defence certificate I report as follows:

1. Nothing to assist the defence, as this is such a broad statement.

2. Exhibits 4,5,6 are transcripts of interview and are evidence at the trial.
On the 18 May 2004 I received a letter from the defence solicitors
requesting a copy of the interview tapes exhibits 1, 2 and 3, I have
arranged for a copy to be sent from Belfast.

I seek permission to forward copies to the defence solicitor. { have a
form PACE24a signed by the solicitor.

3. This would be a trial matter.

4. A Exhibit 49 Item SW42 at pages 242-248 refers. At page 242 there is
what is termed a keying in error of small sums. However there are also
a number of errors including large sums of money contained within this
same exhibit.

8B In relation to manning levels within the shop and Post Office, these
would be the defendant's problem. As she is an agent for the Post
Office she can employ anyone to work in the Post Office at her own
expense.

Form 54/1 Page 1 of 2
S04
PNI00000001_078
PNI00000001_078

C Item 4 of the attached documentation was supplied by Mrs McKelvey to
the Post Office Investigators. This document is Item 4 on this schedule
of unused material. It appears to only refer to goods from the shop and
not the Post Office. As it was supplied by Mrs McKelvey to
investigators she would have to explain in more detail its contents.

D_ Items No 1-5 of the schedule of unused material shows a shortfall of
cash on weeks 26, 33, 44 and 53 which to some extent supports item
No4D of the attached defence schedule.

Susanne Writer from the Post Office can find no record of Mrs McKelvey
requesting further cash to overcome any shortfall, that is, no records
are available at this stage. I Mrs McKelvey could ring the Post Office
Cash Centre and request a special cash remittance which would be
delivered by special delivery within 24 to 48 hours. Again no records of
any such requests are available.

5 There are no manuscript statements. A copy of the notebook entry of
S Writer is attached at Item 3 of the schedule of unused material.

All items in my possession have been supplied to the DPP. I have been
informed by the Post Office that no witness has any relevant
convictions.
Submitted for information and onward transmission to the DPP. A copy of the
correspondence from the DPP is attached.

I have retained all the original items disclosed in this report.

I GRO I

Consignia

EMPLOYEES RIGHTS TOA FRIEND AT A INTERVIEW
INTERVIEWEE:

Consignia has agreed with the Unions that Consignia or SPSO staff when interviewed by an
Investigator may have a friend present at the interview.

Any friend invited to attend a Consignia interview, or search, must be at least 18 years of age and not
already involved in the inquiry. He or she must be a Consignia employee, who may be the local
union representative or other official of the recognised union for the grade. *

Do you require a friend No. ‘

The right t to your right to seek legal advice.

SIGNED MAUREEN MCKELVEY _, TIME AND DATE

to act as a friend during this interview.

Your role as a friend is to withess what happens during the interview but you may not take part in the
interview proceedings.

During the interview you may take notes which must be treated “In Strictest Confidence”. If the
interviewee so requests, at a later stage, you may let him/her have a copy of these notes for use in any
subsequent official appeal about the procedures followed during the interview. If the person being
interviewed so wishes, your statement may be communicated to his/her Union “In Strictest
Confidence”,

No other communication about the interview is allowed without the permission of Consignia.
T have read and understood the above and am willing to act as a friend.

SIGNED

MPLOYEES RIGHTS A FRIEND AT A INTERVIE!

Consignia has agreed with the Unions that Consignia or SPSO staff when interviewed by an
Investigator may have a friend present at the interview.

Any friend invited to attend a Consignia interview, or search, must be at least 18 years of age and not

already involved in the inquiry. He or she must be a Consignia employee, who may be the local
union representative or other official of the recognised union for the grade.

Do you require a friend

If you require a friend, you should write their name here:

The right to a friend is additional to your right to seek legal advice.
